#Debug
add_namespace = goering_debug

country_event = { #Increases militarist power/influence while decreasing loyalty
	id = goering_debug.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering_debug.1"}
	title = goering_debug.1.t
	desc = goering_debug.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_goering_speech

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = goering_debug.1.a
		GGR_decrease_militarist_loyalty_large = yes
		GGR_decrease_militarist_influence_large = yes
		GGR_decrease_militarist_power_large = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Göring wins lol
	id = goering.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.2"}
	title = goering.2.t
	desc = goering.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_goering_speech

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = goering.2.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = { news_event = WORLD.2057 }
		}
	}
}

	}
}

country_event = { # Continue to encroach on Speidel's Germania
	id = goering.38
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.38"}
	title = goering.38.t
	desc = goering.38.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_army

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = goering.38.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = GER
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			HGR = { country_event = { id = HGR.20 days = 1 } }
			BGR = { country_event = { id = bormann.15 days = 1 } }
			SGR = { country_event = { id = speer.26 days = 1 } }
			set_global_flag = GER_Scramble_For_Germania
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = goering.38.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_political_power = -100
		add_stability = -0.1
		transfer_state = 1026
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = goering.39
				days = 25
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = goering.38.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = goering.38
				days = 31
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Göring Dies Naturally
	id = goering.200
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.200"}
	title = goering.200.t
	desc = goering.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_riot

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = goering.200.a
		kill_country_leader = yes
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = despotism
		}
		set_popularities = {
			national_socialism = 50
			ultranationalism = 10
			despotism = 40
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Heinrich Theodore Göring"
			desc = "POLITICS_HEINRICH_THEODORE_GORING_DESC"
			picture = "GER_Portrait_Heinrich_Theodor_Goring.dds"
			expire = "1999.1.1"
			ideology = despotism_military_junta_subtype
		}
	}
	option = { 
		name = goering.200.b
		kill_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Edda Göring"
			desc = "POLITICS_EDDA_GORING_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Germany_Edda_Goring.dds"
			expire = "2018.12.21"
			ideology = national_socialism_subtype
		}
	}
}

		GGR_increase_militarist_loyalty_small = yes

		name = goering.206.b

		GGR_decrease_militarist_loyalty = yes
	}
	option = {

		set_country_flag = GGR_CIND_apolitical_man
		add_political_power = -25
		GGR_decrease_militarist_influence_small = yes
		GGR_decrease_militarist_loyalty_small = yes
	}
}

country_event = {	
	id = goering.208
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.208"}
	title = goering.208.t

	desc = {    
		text = goering.208.desc_militarists_man
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GGR_CIND_militarists_man
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = goering.208.desc_goering_man
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GGR_CIND_goering_man
		}
	}
	
	desc = {
		text = goering.208.desc_apolitical_man
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GGR_CIND_apolitical_man
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_army
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Modern Führerbunker with War Room
		name = goering.208.a

			has_country_flag = GGR_CIND_militarists_man
		}
		set_temp_variable = { debt_temp = 0.5 }
		econ_national_debt_change = yes

		GGR_increase_militarist_power_large = yes
		64 = {

# New Missile Designs
country_event = {	
	id = goering.210
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.210"}
	title = goering.210.t
	desc = goering.210.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_german_army
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Total rearm
		name = goering.210.a
		set_temp_variable = { debt_temp = 0.4 }
		econ_national_debt_change = yes
		add_to_variable = {
			nuclear_stockpile_change = 30
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = goering.210.a.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { days = 300 id = goering.211 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Slow update
		name = goering.210.b
		set_temp_variable = { debt_temp = 0.25 }
		econ_national_debt_change = yes
		add_to_variable = {
			nuclear_stockpile_change = 10
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = goering.210.b.tt		
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { days = 550 id = goering.211 }
		}
	}
}

		set_temp_variable = { money_reserves_temp = 0.75 }
		econ_money_reserves_change_raw_money = yes
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = missile_silo
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = ICBM_equipment
			amount = 250
			producer = GER
		}	
		
	}
}

country_event = {	#Damaged Reactor Event Start
	id = goering.327
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.327"
		hidden_effect = { GGRCSI_increase_public_concern = yes }
	}
	title = goering.327.t
	desc = goering.327.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MAD_palace

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#Fix it
		name = goering.327.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { nuclear_maintenance > 50 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_Good_Fix_Reactor
		custom_effect_tooltip = GGR_nuclear_maintenance_increase_30
		set_temp_variable = { debt_temp = 4 }
		econ_national_debt_change = yes
		add_to_variable = { nuclear_maintenance = 30 }
		55 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = nuclear_reactor
				damage = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Knock it down the line
		name = goering.327.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_No_Fix_Reactor

			limit = { has_country_flag = GGR_speidels_victory }
			clr_country_flag = GGR_speidels_victory

			set_country_flag = GGR_speidels_victory

	}
}

			has_war = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}

	}

	id = goering.821
	title = goering.821.t
	desc = goering.821.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MAD_palace

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.821"}

	option = {
		name = goering.821.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { GGR_GDP_collapse = GDP }
					check_variable = { GGR_GDP_collapse > GDP }
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = goering.822 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Its all over now
	id = goering.822
	title = goering.822.t
	desc = goering.822.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MAD_palace

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.822"}
	
	option = {
		name = goering.822.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = GER
			}
			GER = {
				white_peace = PREV
			}
		}
		add_ideas = GGR_total_economic_collapse
		clr_country_flag = GGR_economy_tree
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_GDP_boost_flat = -30 }
		econ_GDP_boost_once_flat = yes
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = -1 } 
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		add_to_variable = { interest_rates = 2 }
		country_event = {
			id = goering_schoerner.1 days = 1 
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_GOR_Militarists_mad
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Militarist_Loyalty = 30 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Militarist_Influence = 30 }
	
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = GER_war_plan_A
			clr_country_flag = GER_war_plan_B
			clr_country_flag = GER_war_plan_C
			clr_country_flag = GGR_economy_tree
			clr_country_flag = GGR_military_tree
			clr_country_flag = GGR_science_tree
			GGR_Reload_main = yes
		}
	}
	#option = {
	#	name = goering.822.a
	#	set_country_flag = TNO_closing_screen_show

country_event = { # Old friends
	id = goering.1043
	title = goering.1043.t
	desc = goering.1043.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MAD_palace

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.1043"}

	option = {
		# Bulgaria = ally 
		name = goering.1043.a
		add_to_faction = BUL

		send_equipment = {
			target = BUL
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 250
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = BUL
			type = artillery_equipment
			amount = 120
		}
		BUL = {
			add_manpower = 40000
		}
		GER = {
			add_manpower = -40000
		}
	}
	option = {
		# Absorb Bulgaria into RKB
		name = goering.1043.b
		RKB = {
			econ_join_sphere_GER = yes
			annex_country = {
				target = BUL
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = BUL 
				}
				RKB = {
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		send_equipment = {
			target = RKB
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 250
		}
		send_equipment = {
			target = RKB
			type = artillery_equipment
			amount = 120
		}
		RKB = {
			add_ideas = Pakt_Autonomous_Reichskommissariat
			add_manpower = 40000
		}
		GER = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = RKB
				autonomy_state = autonomy_autonomous_reichskommissariat
			}
			add_to_faction = RKB
			add_manpower = -40000
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.1055"}

	option = { # Keep it in our territory
		name = goering.1055.a
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					country_event = { id = goering.1050 days = 5 }
				}
				1 = {
					country_event = { id = goering.1051 days = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Drop us in chief!
		name = goering.1055.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { infiltration_succes_chance = random }
			add_to_temp_variable = { infiltration_succes_chance = GGR_luftwaffe_para_attack }
			add_to_temp_variable = { infiltration_succes_chance = GGR_luftwaffe_accident_chance }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { infiltration_succes_chance > 0.69 } }
				country_event = { id = goering.1056 days = 5 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = goering.1057 days = 5 }
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = goering_peace_events.1.a
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = MCW_collapse
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = MCW }
			GGR_increase_militarist_power_small = yes
			GGR_increase_militarist_influence_small = yes
		}
		else = {
			GGR_decrease_military_industrial_participation = yes
		}
	}
}

				}
			}
		}

country_event = { #US
	id = goering_anti.4
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering_anti.4"}
	title = goering_anti.4.t
	desc = goering_anti.4.desc
	#picture =

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = goering_anti.4.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 2 }
		anti_goering_send_equipment = yes
		anti_goering_send_volunteers = yes

		event_target:GGR_Defender = {
			country_event = { id = goering_anti.6 days = 1 }
			set_country_flag = USA_entered_war
		}

		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = USA
				NOT = { original_tag = USA }
			}
			country_event = { id = goering_anti.7 }
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = GGR_ignore_enemy_aid_events
						}
					}
				}
				GER = {
					country_event = { id = goering_anti.5 days = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #
		name = goering_anti.4.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		anti_goering_send_equipment = yes
		send_equipment = {
			equipment = anti_tank_equipment_1
			amount = 1000
			target = event_target:GGR_Defender
		}

		event_target:GGR_Defender = {
			country_event = { id = goering_anti.6 days = 1 }
		}

		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = USA
				NOT = { original_tag = USA }
			}
			country_event = { id = goering_anti.7 }
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = GGR_ignore_enemy_aid_events
						}
					}
				}
				GER = {
					country_event = { id = goering_anti.5 days = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #
		name = goering_anti.4.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = USA
			}
			country_event = { id = goering_anti.8 }
		}
	}
}

	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = goering_japan_interaction.14.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP	 = {
					check_variable = {
						var = GER_JAP_suspicion
						value = 10
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			GER = {
				country_event = { days = 1 id = goering_japan_interaction.17 } }
			JAP = {
				country_event = { days = 1 id = goering_japan_interaction.34 } }
			set_global_flag = GER_GOR_CHI_Alliance
		}
		else = {
			GER = {
				country_event = { days = 1 id = goering_japan_interaction.15 } }
			set_global_flag = GER_GOR_CHI_Alliance
		}
	}
	option = { #No
		name = goering_japan_interaction.14.b
		GER = {
			country_event = { days = 1 id = goering_japan_interaction.16 } }
	}
}

					id = goering.521
					days = 10
				}

					country_event = {
						id = goering.524
						days = 10
					}
				}
			}

				country_event = {
					id = goering.522
					days = 10
				}
				PER  = {
					country_event = {
						id = goering.523
						days = 10
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	#It worked
	id = goering.185
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.185"}
	title = goering.185.t
	desc = goering.185.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_mlk_assassinated

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {	#great news!"
		name = goering.185.a
		CUB = {
			kill_country_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					CUB = {
						has_civil_war = no
					}
				}
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = fascism
					size = 0.20
					capital = 1236
					states = { 1236 1309 }
					states = { 1308 1237 }
				}
				else = {
					random_country = {
						limit = {
							original_tag = CUB
							has_government = fascism
						}
						add_manpower = 7500
						add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
							type = infantry_equipment
							amount = 10000
							producer = GER
						}
					}
					CUB = {
						add_manpower = -5000
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

						}

							limit = {
								has_country_flag = BOP_SUPPORT
							}

						}
					}

				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # Supply depot activation
	id = goering.1479
	title = goering.1479.t
	desc = goering.1479.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_army2

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.1479"}

	option = {
		name = goering.1479.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GGR_weak_supply_depots
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = GGR_supply_depots
				add_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { GGR_supply_depot_weakened }
					province = {
						all_provinces = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		else = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = GGR_supply_depots
				add_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { GGR_supply_depot }
					province = {
						all_provinces = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = goering.1480 days = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { # Its all over now
	id = goering.505052
	title = goering.505052.t
	desc = goering.505052.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_MAD_palace

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event goering.505052"}
	
	option = {
		name = goering.505052.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = GER
			}
			GER = {
				white_peace = PREV
			}
		}
		add_ideas = GGR_total_economic_collapse
		clr_country_flag = GGR_economy_tree
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_GDP_boost_flat = -30 }
		econ_GDP_boost_once_flat = yes
		subtract_from_variable = { GDP_growth = -0.05 }
		add_to_variable = { interest_rates = 2 }
		country_event = { id = goering_schoerner.1 days = 4 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_GOR_Militarists_mad
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Militarist_Loyalty = 30 }

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = goering.505053 days = 2 }
			clr_country_flag = GER_war_plan_A
			clr_country_flag = GER_war_plan_B
			clr_country_flag = GER_war_plan_C
			clr_country_flag = GGR_economy_tree
			clr_country_flag = GGR_military_tree
			clr_country_flag = GGR_science_tree
			GGR_Reload_main = yes
		}
		ENG = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ENG_sealion }
				remove_mission = ENG_DEC_USA_equipment_sealion
				clr_country_flag = ENG_sealion_guns
				if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = ENG_GF_WonECW }
					country_event = ENG_sealion.4 
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = FEN_GF_WonECW }
					country_event = ENG_sealion.103 
				}
			}
		}
	}
